<p><b>Paulo Bruno Exequiel Dybala</b> (<small>Spanish pronunciation:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">[paulo ðiala]</a></span>;<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;A&#93;</a></sup> born 15 November 1993) is an Argentine professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a> for <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> club <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina national team</a>. Considered one of the world's most valuable players,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;B&#93;</a></sup> he is commonly referred to as "<i>La Joya</i>" ("The Jewel") due to his creative style of play, pace, talent, technique and eye for goal.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Palermitans also refer to him as "U Picciriddu" ("The Kid" in the <a href="/wiki/Sicilian_language" title="Sicilian language">Sicilian dialect</a>), because of his young age at the time of his signing for <a href="/wiki/S.S.D._Palermo" class="mw-redirect" title="S.S.D. Palermo">Palermo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After beginning his career in Argentina with <a href="/wiki/Instituto_Atl%C3%A9tico_Central_C%C3%B3rdoba" title="Instituto Atlético Central Córdoba">Instituto de Córdoba</a> in 2011, Dybala moved to Italian club <a href="/wiki/U.S._Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Città di Palermo">Palermo</a> in 2012. He played three seasons for Palermo, two in <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> and one <a href="/wiki/Serie_B" title="Serie B">Serie B</a> in <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Serie_B" title="2013–14 Serie B">2013–14</a>. In 2015, he joined Juventus for an initial fee of €32 million and has since made over 100 appearances for the club, winning the <a href="/wiki/Double_(association_football)" title="Double (association football)">double</a> of Serie A and <a href="/wiki/Coppa_Italia" title="Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a> in his first three seasons, as well as two more consecutive league titles, and two <a href="/wiki/Supercoppa_Italiana" title="Supercoppa Italiana">Supercoppa Italiana</a> titles. He has also been named in the <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Team_of_the_Year" title="Serie A Team of the Year">Serie A Team of the Year</a> three times and won the <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Awards" title="Serie A Awards">Most Valuable Player</a> award for the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Serie_A" title="2019–20 Serie A">2019–20</a> season.
</p><p>Dybala made his senior international debut for Argentina in 2015, representing his nation at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> and the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 Copa América</a>. In the latter tournament, he scored the game-winner to help his nation finish in third-place.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Dybala was born in Laguna Larga, <a href="/wiki/C%C3%B3rdoba_Province,_Argentina" title="Córdoba Province, Argentina">Córdoba</a>, Argentina.<sup id="cite_ref-The_Cordoba_Connection_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_Cordoba_Connection-9">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> His grandfather, Bolesaw Dybaa, was from the village of <a href="/wiki/Kra%C5%9Bni%C3%B3w" title="Kraniów">Kraniów</a> in Poland; he fled from his country of birth to Argentina during <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Metà_polacco_e_metà_italiano_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Metà_polacco_e_metà_italiano-10">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-dybala_newmessi_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dybala_newmessi-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Some of his grandfather's family moved to Canada.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Dybala's family also has Italian origins through his maternal great-grandmother, whose surname was Da Messa, from the <a href="/wiki/Province_of_Naples" title="Province of Naples">Province of Naples</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Metà_polacco_e_metà_italiano_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Metà_polacco_e_metà_italiano-10">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-noitalian_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-noitalian-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-dybala_italian_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dybala_italian-14">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Dybala obtained Italian citizenship on 13 August 2012,<sup id="cite_ref-Dybala_è_cittadino_italiano_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dybala_è_cittadino_italiano-16">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> in order to facilitate his move to <a href="/wiki/Palermo_F.C." title="Palermo F.C.">Palermo F.C.</a><sup id="cite_ref-:0_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-17">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> and circumvent <a href="/wiki/Italian_Football_Federation" title="Italian Football Federation">FIGC</a> regulations that permit only a maximum of two non-<a href="/wiki/Citizenship_of_the_European_Union" title="Citizenship of the European Union">EU</a> players in any <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> team.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Dybala initially attempted to obtain Polish citizenship through ancestry from his grandfather, but the bureaucracy proved too complex.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-17">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Dybala is the youngest of three brothers and lost his father in 2008 to cancer.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Instituto_de_C.C3.B3rdoba"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Instituto_de_Córdoba">Instituto de Córdoba</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Instituto de Córdoba">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Nicknamed "<i>La Joya</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-dybala_lajoya_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dybala_lajoya-19">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> or "<i>El pibe de la pensión</i>",<sup id="cite_ref-dybala_elpibedelapension_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dybala_elpibedelapension-20">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Dybala made his professional debut in the <a href="/wiki/Primera_B_Nacional" class="mw-redirect" title="Primera B Nacional">Primera B Nacional</a> (Argentine second division) with his hometown club <a href="/wiki/Instituto_Atl%C3%A9tico_Central_C%C3%B3rdoba" title="Instituto Atlético Central Córdoba">Instituto Atlético Central Córdoba</a> at age 17. In total, he played 40 matches with the club, scoring 17 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-SW_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-21">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-dybala_player2_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dybala_player2-22">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> He was the youngest to score a goal, beating the record of <a href="/wiki/Mario_Kempes" title="Mario Kempes">Mario Kempes</a>. Dybala was also the first to play 38 consecutive matches in a professional league in the country (again edging Kempes), and was also the first to score two hat-tricks in a season. Dybala also scored in six consecutive games, surpassing the previous record of four matches.<sup id="cite_ref-dybala_record_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dybala_record-23">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Palermo">Palermo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Palermo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Paulo_Dybala_-_2015_-_US_Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo_(corner_kick).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Paulo_Dybala_-_2015_-_US_Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo_%28corner_kick%29.jpg/220px-Paulo_Dybala_-_2015_-_US_Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo_%28corner_kick%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Paulo_Dybala_-_2015_-_US_Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo_%28corner_kick%29.jpg/330px-Paulo_Dybala_-_2015_-_US_Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo_%28corner_kick%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Paulo_Dybala_-_2015_-_US_Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo_%28corner_kick%29.jpg/440px-Paulo_Dybala_-_2015_-_US_Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo_%28corner_kick%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1199" data-file-height="1199" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Paulo_Dybala_-_2015_-_US_Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo_(corner_kick).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Dybala taking a corner for <a href="/wiki/U.S._Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Città di Palermo">Palermo</a> in 2015</div></div></div>
<p>On 29 April 2012, <a href="/wiki/U.S._Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Città di Palermo">U.S. Città di Palermo</a> president <a href="/wiki/Maurizio_Zamparini" title="Maurizio Zamparini">Maurizio Zamparini</a> announced the signing of Dybala stating, "We have got Paulo Dybala – the new <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Sergio Agüero</a>."<sup id="cite_ref-dybala_aguero_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dybala_aguero-24">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Later the same day, however, Instituto's general secretary José Teaux stated that the man who had completed the negotiations with Palermo did not have the mandate to sell Dybala. Nonetheless, on 20 July 2012 Palermo released a press announcement confirming the signing of Dybala, who signed a four-year deal with the Sicilian club.<sup id="cite_ref-dybala_signed_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dybala_signed-25">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> According to the financial filing of the club, the transfer fee was €8.64&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Dybala made his debut for the club in a <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> match against <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a>. He scored his first and second goal in Italy on 11 November 2012 when Palermo defeated <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a> at home, 2–0.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Dybala had his breakthrough season in the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Serie_A" title="2014–15 Serie A">2014–15 Serie A</a> where he scored ten goals in the first half of the season, forming a successful striking partnership with fellow Argentine–Italian <a href="/wiki/Franco_V%C3%A1zquez" title="Franco Vázquez">Franco Vázquez</a> and being linked with several top European clubs.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> He finished the season with 13 goals and 10 assists, which made him one of the top assist providers in the league.<sup id="cite_ref-espnfc.com_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espnfc.com-29">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Juventus">Juventus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Juventus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–16_season">2015–16 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2015–16 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 4 June 2015, <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> announced the signing of Dybala on a five-year deal for a fee of €32&#160;million (plus €8&#160;million in add-ons).<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> He was assigned the number 21 shirt, previously worn by <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Pirlo" title="Andrea Pirlo">Andrea Pirlo</a>, who left the club that summer.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> On 8 August, he came on as a 61st-minute substitute for <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Coman" title="Kingsley Coman">Kingsley Coman</a> against Lazio in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2015 Supercoppa Italiana">2015 Supercoppa Italiana</a>. He scored the second goal in the 73rd minute in a 2–0 win in <a href="/wiki/Shanghai" title="Shanghai">Shanghai</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> On 30 August 2015, Dybala scored his first league goal for the club in the 87th minute in a 2–1 defeat to <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> In his first 16 appearances of the season, Dybala managed six goals and two assists in all competitions, with a ratio of a goal every 151 minutes, which was superior to <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Tevez" title="Carlos Tevez">Carlos Tevez</a>'s and <a href="/wiki/Alessandro_Del_Piero" title="Alessandro Del Piero">Alessandro Del Piero</a>'s goalscoring ratios in their debut seasons with Juventus. In the club's history, only <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Baggio" title="Roberto Baggio">Roberto Baggio</a> maintained a superior goalscoring record in the opening games of his debut season.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Dybala scored his first career <a href="/wiki/Coppa_Italia" title="Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a> goal in a 4–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Derby_della_Mole" title="Derby della Mole">cross-city rivals</a> <a href="/wiki/Torino_F.C." title="Torino F.C.">Torino</a> on 16 December.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> On 23 February 2016, Dybala scored his first <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> goal in a 2–2 home draw to <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> in Juventus' first round of 16 leg.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> On 15 March, it was announced Dybala would miss the second round of 16 leg of the Champions League against Bayern on 16 March due to an edema overload of his left <a href="/wiki/Soleus_muscle" title="Soleus muscle">soleus muscle</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> He returned to action four days later in a 4–1 away win over Torino,<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> but was substituted after sustaining yet another injury.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> On 21 April, Dybala scored two goals in a 3–0 home win over Lazio, which took his league tally to 16 goals in 31 appearances and also saw him score his 20th goal of the season in all competitions in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> He finished the season as Juventus' top scorer with 23 goals in all competitions and 19 goals in Serie A, as the club celebrated their Serie A title victory.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–17_season">2016–17 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2016–17 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Dybala_2017_(edited).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Dybala_2017_%28edited%29.jpg/170px-Dybala_2017_%28edited%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="240" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Dybala_2017_%28edited%29.jpg/255px-Dybala_2017_%28edited%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Dybala_2017_%28edited%29.jpg/340px-Dybala_2017_%28edited%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2030" data-file-height="2870" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Dybala_2017_(edited).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Dybala with <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> in 2017</div></div></div>
<p>Following the departure of <a href="/wiki/Paul_Pogba" title="Paul Pogba">Paul Pogba</a> to <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> in the summer of 2016, Dybala was offered the <a href="/wiki/Number_10_jersey" class="mw-redirect" title="Number 10 jersey">number 10 jersey</a> by Juventus, although he turned it down, preferring to keep the number 21 jersey that he had worn during his previous season.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Following manager <a href="/wiki/Massimiliano_Allegri" title="Massimiliano Allegri">Massimiliano Allegri</a>'s switch to a <a href="/wiki/Formation_(association_football)#4–2–3–1" title="Formation (association football)">4–2–3–1 formation</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Juventus_F.C._season" title="2016–17 Juventus F.C. season">2016–17 season</a> saw Dybala operate in a deeper playmaking role behind the club's new signing <a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_Higua%C3%ADn" title="Gonzalo Higuaín">Gonzalo Higuaín</a>, which saw a decrease in his goalscoring output as he took on increasing defensive and creative duties.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> After struggling to score at the beginning of the season, Dybala scored his first goal of the 2016–17 campaign on 27 September, in a 4–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/GNK_Dinamo_Zagreb" title="GNK Dinamo Zagreb">Dinamo Zagreb</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Serie_A" title="2016–17 Serie A">Serie A</a> goal of the season that weekend, on 2 October, in a 3–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/Empoli_F.C." title="Empoli F.C.">Empoli</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 April, Dybala scored two goals in Juventus's first-leg Champions League quarter-final fixture against Barcelona, helping the club to a 3–0 home victory.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> On 13 April 2017, Dybala renewed his contract with Juventus until 2022.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On 3 June, Dybala started in the <a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2017 UEFA Champions League Final">2017 Champions League Final</a>, but Juventus were defeated 4–1 by defending champions <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a>, missing out on the treble.<sup id="cite_ref-Guardian_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-52">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18_season">2017–18 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2017–18 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 4 August 2017, Dybala was named one of the three finalists for the Forward of the 2016–17 UEFA Champions League season award.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On 9 August, Dybala was confirmed to wear the number 10 shirt for Juventus.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On 13 August he scored two goals in a 3–2 defeat to Lazio in the <a href="/wiki/2017_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2017 Supercoppa Italiana">2017 Supercoppa Italiana</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> On 15 August, Dybala placed sixth in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Best_Player_in_Europe_Award#2016.E2.80.9317" class="mw-redirect" title="UEFA Best Player in Europe Award">2017 UEFA Best Player of the Year Award</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> On 26 August, Dybala scored his first hat-trick in Serie A in a 4–2 away win over <a href="/wiki/Genoa_C.F.C." title="Genoa C.F.C.">Genoa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> He repeated the feat on 17 September, in his 100th appearance for Juventus, scoring all three goals, including one free-kick, in the club's 3–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/U.S._Sassuolo_Calcio" title="U.S. Sassuolo Calcio">Sassuolo</a>, marking his second hat-trick in Serie A.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> On 11 March 2018, Dybala scored a brace in a 2–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/Udinese_Calcio" title="Udinese Calcio">Udinese</a> in Serie A; his first goal of the match was also his 100th career goal.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> He made his 150th appearance in Serie A in a 0–0 away draw against <a href="/wiki/S.P.A.L._2013" class="mw-redirect" title="S.P.A.L. 2013">S.P.A.L.</a>, on 17 March.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19_season">2018–19 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2018–19 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 1 September 2018, Dybala made his 100th Serie A appearance for Juventus, coming on as a late second-half substitute in a 2–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/Parma_F._C." class="mw-redirect" title="Parma F. C.">Parma</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> On 2 October, Dybala scored a <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> in a 3–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/BSC_Young_Boys" title="BSC Young Boys">Young Boys</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> In Juventus's following Champions League group match on 23 October, Dybala scored the only goal of the game in a 1–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> With the arrival of <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>, Dybala was often deployed out of position in a deeper role by manager Allegri during the 2018–19 season; as a result of this positional switch, as well as struggles with injuries, and difficulties with his manager, Dybala suffered a loss of form, and his goalscoring output decreased significantly, as he managed to score only five goals in 30 league matches, and 10 goals across 42 appearances in all competitions. However, Juventus managed to retain the Serie A title.<sup id="cite_ref-swap_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-swap-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-plug_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-plug-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20_season">2019–20 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 2019–20 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Following a disappointing 2018–19 campaign, Dybala was initially linked with moves to <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> sides <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham</a>, although he ultimately remained with Juventus for the 2019–20 season.<sup id="cite_ref-swap_65-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-swap-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-plug_66-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-plug-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-reason_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-reason-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Although he was initially not expected to start under the club's new manager <a href="/wiki/Maurizio_Sarri" title="Maurizio Sarri">Maurizio Sarri</a>, he eventually broke into the first XI and scored his first goal of the season on 6 October 2019, in a 2–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/Derby_d%27Italia" title="Derby d&#39;Italia">rivals</a> <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter</a>, to help his side overtake the <i>Nerazzurri</i> at the top of the Serie A table.<sup id="cite_ref-reason_67-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-reason-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> On 7 December, he made his 200th appearance for Juventus in a 3–1 away defeat to Lazio in Serie A.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2020_Coppa_Italia_Final" title="2020 Coppa Italia Final">2020 Coppa Italia Final</a> against <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a> on 17 June, following a 0–0 draw after regulation time, Dybala missed Juventus's first spot-kick in the resulting shoot-out, with his shot being saved by <a href="/wiki/Alex_Meret" title="Alex Meret">Alex Meret</a>; Napoli ultimately won the match 4–2 on penalties.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the end of the season, Dybala was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Awards" title="Serie A Awards">Serie A MVP award</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Serie_A" title="2019–20 Serie A">2019–20 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Serie_A_Awards_2019–20_71-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Serie_A_Awards_2019–20-71">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> He finished the campaign with 11 goals and 6 assists, helping Juventus win their 9th consecutive title.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 2020–21 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 20 October 2020, Dybala made his first appearance of the season in Juventus's opening <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2020–21 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> game, coming on as a second–half substitute in a 2–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Dynamo_Kyiv" title="FC Dynamo Kyiv">Dynamo Kyiv</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> Dybala scored his first goal of the season on 4 November against <a href="/wiki/Ferencv%C3%A1rosi_TC" title="Ferencvárosi TC">Ferencváros</a> in a 4–1 win during a Champions League group stage match.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:132px;"><a href="/wiki/File:2017_FRIENDLY_MATCH_RUSSIA_v_ARGENTINA_-_Paulo_Dybala_02.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/2017_FRIENDLY_MATCH_RUSSIA_v_ARGENTINA_-_Paulo_Dybala_02.jpg/130px-2017_FRIENDLY_MATCH_RUSSIA_v_ARGENTINA_-_Paulo_Dybala_02.jpg" decoding="async" width="130" height="336" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/2017_FRIENDLY_MATCH_RUSSIA_v_ARGENTINA_-_Paulo_Dybala_02.jpg/195px-2017_FRIENDLY_MATCH_RUSSIA_v_ARGENTINA_-_Paulo_Dybala_02.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/2017_FRIENDLY_MATCH_RUSSIA_v_ARGENTINA_-_Paulo_Dybala_02.jpg/260px-2017_FRIENDLY_MATCH_RUSSIA_v_ARGENTINA_-_Paulo_Dybala_02.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1148" data-file-height="2968" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:2017_FRIENDLY_MATCH_RUSSIA_v_ARGENTINA_-_Paulo_Dybala_02.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Dybala playing for Argentina against <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_football_team" title="Russia national football team">Russia</a> in 2017</div></div></div>
<p>Due to his family heritage, Dybala was eligible to play for <a href="/wiki/Poland_national_football_team" title="Poland national football team">Poland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a>, but expressly stated that he feels Argentine and had always dreamed of playing for <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> Dybala stated "I feel 100 percent Argentinian, I wouldn't be happy in a national team that didn't feel like mine, to hear an anthem that isn't my own, in colours that don't belong to me".<sup id="cite_ref-noitalian_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-noitalian-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Dybala was called by the <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_under-17_football_team" title="Argentina national under-17 football team">Argentina under-17 team</a> to participate in the <a href="/wiki/2011_Pan_American_Games" title="2011 Pan American Games">XVI Pan American Games</a>, but ultimately did not take part in the competition. On 19 July 2012, he received his first call-up for the <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_under-20_football_team" title="Argentina national under-20 football team">under-20 team</a>, but declined the invitation.
</p><p>On 22 September 2015, Dybala was called for the first time for the Argentina senior team by manager <a href="/wiki/Gerardo_Martino" title="Gerardo Martino">Gerardo Martino</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> but his first appearance was on 13 October 2015, coming off the bench to replace Carlos Tevez in the 75th minute during a <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONMEBOL)" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (CONMEBOL)">2018 FIFA World Cup qualifying</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Paraguay_national_football_team" title="Paraguay national football team">Paraguay</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> In May 2016, he was omitted from Argentina's 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Centenario" title="Copa América Centenario">Copa América Centenario</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> Although Juventus insisted that they would not release Dybala for the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2016 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">2016 Summer Olympics</a> in <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a>, he was included in Martino's 35-man preliminary <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_under-23_football_team" title="Argentina national under-23 football team">under-23 squad</a> for the tournament on 24 May;<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> he was not included in the final squad for the tournament, however.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 1 September 2016, Dybala was sent off in the first half of a 1–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a> in a 2018 World Cup qualifier for a second bookable offence.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> On 13 June 2017, he set up a goal for <a href="/wiki/Joaqu%C3%ADn_Correa" title="Joaquín Correa">Joaquín Correa</a> in a 6–0 away friendly win over <a href="/wiki/Singapore_national_football_team" title="Singapore national football team">Singapore</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2018, Dybala was named in Argentina's preliminary 35-man <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> in Russia;<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> later that month, he was included in <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Sampaoli" title="Jorge Sampaoli">Jorge Sampaoli</a>'s final 23-man squad for the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> He made his World Cup debut in Argentina's second group match on 21 June, coming on as a second-half substitute for <a href="/wiki/Enzo_P%C3%A9rez" title="Enzo Pérez">Enzo Pérez</a> in the 68th minute of an eventual 3–0 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> This was his only appearance in the tournament, as Argentina were eliminated in the round of 16 on 30 June, following a 4–3 defeat to <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later that year, he scored his first senior international goal on 20 November, in a 2–0 friendly home win over <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_football_team" title="Mexico national football team">Mexico</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2019, Dybala was included in Argentina manager <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Scaloni" title="Lionel Scaloni">Lionel Scaloni</a>'s preliminary 40-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 Copa América</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> Later that month, he was included in the final 23-man squad for the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> In Argentina's final group match against <a href="/wiki/Qatar_national_football_team" title="Qatar national football team">Qatar</a> on 23 June, Dybala assisted Agüero's goal in a 2–0 win after coming off the bench for <a href="/wiki/Lautaro_Mart%C3%ADnez" title="Lautaro Martínez">Lautaro Martínez</a>, which enabled them to advance to the knock-out stages of the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> In the third-place match against <a href="/wiki/Chile_national_football_team" title="Chile national football team">Chile</a> on 6 July, Dybala made his first start of the tournament, and scored Argentina's second goal in an eventual 2–1 win, to help his team capture the bronze medal.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A quick, creative, elegant, and agile player, with excellent technical ability and a low centre of gravity,<sup id="cite_ref-evolution_and_devolution_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-evolution_and_devolution-93">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-uefa.com_94-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-uefa.com-94">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Inter,_ecco_baby_Dybala_98-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Inter,_ecco_baby_Dybala-98">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> Dybala is known for his powerful and accurate shots from outside the box, <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> skills, balance, and close control in limited spaces,<sup id="cite_ref-Inter,_ecco_baby_Dybala_98-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Inter,_ecco_baby_Dybala-98">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo_100-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo-100">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> as well as his ability to beat opponents in one on one situations and protect or hold up the ball for teammates with his back to goal.<sup id="cite_ref-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo_100-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo-100">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> Due to his speed on the ball, positioning, intelligent movement, and ball skills, he excels during counter-attacks<sup id="cite_ref-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo_100-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo-100">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> and at beating the offside trap when making attacking runs.<sup id="cite_ref-Scouting_Report_101-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scouting_Report-101">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-blank_102-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-blank-102">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> A hardworking player, he is also known for his stamina and defensive contribution off the ball.<sup id="cite_ref-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo_100-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo-100">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-elite_103-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-elite-103">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> Dybala is capable both of creating chances for teammates, as well as scoring goals himself, due to his vision, passing, link-up play, and ability to drop deep and play off of other players, as well as his powerful and accurate ball-striking ability from both inside and outside the area.<sup id="cite_ref-Scouting_Report_101-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scouting_Report-101">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-blank_102-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-blank-102">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-elite_103-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-elite-103">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-How_Juventus_miss_Dybala_104-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_Juventus_miss_Dybala-104">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> Despite his diminutive stature, Dybala is also effective at scoring with his head, due to his acceleration over short distances, and his ability to anticipate defenders inside the box.<sup id="cite_ref-Inter,_ecco_baby_Dybala_98-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Inter,_ecco_baby_Dybala-98">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo_100-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo-100">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A versatile <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a>, he is capable of playing in any offensive position: he started out playing as a left winger for Instituto in Argentina towards the beginning of his career,<sup id="cite_ref-evolution_and_devolution_93-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-evolution_and_devolution-93">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> but since moving to Italy he has been deployed in a variety of attacking roles, including as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Striker" title="Forward (association football)">main striker</a>, as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Centre-forward" title="Forward (association football)">centre-forward</a>, as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Second_striker" title="Forward (association football)">supporting forward</a>, as an <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">attacking midfielder</a>, in a free role as a wide <a href="/wiki/Playmaker" title="Playmaker">playmaker</a>, as a right-sided <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Inside_forward" title="Forward (association football)">inside forward</a>, as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#False_attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">false attacking midfielder</a>, as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#False_9" title="Forward (association football)">false-9</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-evolution_and_devolution_93-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-evolution_and_devolution-93">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-How_Juventus_miss_Dybala_104-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_Juventus_miss_Dybala-104">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Dybala_tra_Sivori_e_Tevez_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dybala_tra_Sivori_e_Tevez-106">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-faccio_tutto_108-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-faccio_tutto-108">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> or even as an <a href="/wiki/Inverted_Winger" class="mw-redirect" title="Inverted Winger">inverted</a> <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Winger" title="Forward (association football)">winger</a> on the right flank, where he is able to cut into the centre and <a href="/wiki/Curl_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Curl (football)">curl</a> shots on goal with his stronger left foot.<sup id="cite_ref-Inter,_ecco_baby_Dybala_98-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Inter,_ecco_baby_Dybala-98">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo_100-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paulo_Dybala,_17_gol_per_stregare_il_Palermo-100">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-faccio_tutto_108-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-faccio_tutto-108">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> He has also been used in a free attacking role on occasion, in which he is given licence to roam about the final third of the pitch, and either drop into the middle, or switch between the flanks, due to his ability to create from the left or cut inside and score from the right.<sup id="cite_ref-evolution_and_devolution_93-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-evolution_and_devolution-93">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> Because of his work-rate and involvement in the build-up of his team's attacking plays, in addition to his goalscoring ability, former Juventus manager Massimiliano Allegri even deployed Dybala as an offensive-minded <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central midfielder</a> on occasion (known as a "<a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Mezzala" title="Midfielder">mezz'ala</a>", in Italian),<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> and described him as a "<a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Box-to-box_midfielder" title="Midfielder">box-to-box player</a>" ("tuttocampista", in Italian) in 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> He has also operated in a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Deep-lying_playmaker" title="Midfielder">deeper playmaking role</a> on occasion.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> Dybala is also accurate from both <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct free kick">free kicks</a> and <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalties</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> His playing style has drawn comparisons with compatriots Sergio Agüero,<sup id="cite_ref-dybala_aguero_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dybala_aguero-24">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Javier_Pastore" title="Javier Pastore">Javier Pastore</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> Carlos Tevez,<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Omar_S%C3%ADvori" title="Omar Sívori">Omar Sívori</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/New_Maradona" title="New Maradona">Diego</a> <a href="/wiki/Diego_Maradona" title="Diego Maradona">Maradona</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-uefa.com_94-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-uefa.com-94">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> as well as former Italian forwards <a href="/wiki/Vincenzo_Montella" title="Vincenzo Montella">Vincenzo Montella</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-dybala_montella_120-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dybala_montella-120">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> Alessandro Del Piero,<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Baggio" title="Roberto Baggio">Roberto Baggio</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> the latter described Dybala as the number 10 of the future in 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> Widely considered to be a highly talented prospect in world football,<sup id="cite_ref-blank_102-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-blank-102">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-elite_103-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-elite-103">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup> in 2014, <i><a href="/wiki/Don_Bal%C3%B3n" title="Don Balón">Don Balón</a></i> named him one of the 100 most promising young players in the world born after 1993.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> Despite his talent, however, his mentality, consistency, and leadership qualities have come into question at times in the media.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After scoring a goal, Dybala is known for using his signature "mask" <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">celebration</a>; regarding the gesture, he commented: "My mask gesture isn't so much a goal celebration but rather a message. It's an ideal mask, which gladiators wore to fight. In Doha against Milan, after we lost Supercoppa, the idea of this celebration was born."<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Dybala has several tattoos on his body: two stripes on his left arm, an Arabic tattoo as well as a crowned football on his leg.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> On 21 March 2020, Dybala and his girlfriend, <a href="/wiki/Oriana_Sabatini" title="Oriana Sabatini">Oriana Sabatini</a>, tested positive for <a href="/wiki/Coronavirus_disease_2019" class="mw-redirect" title="Coronavirus disease 2019">COVID-19</a>, amid its <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_Italy" title="COVID-19 pandemic in Italy">pandemic in Italy</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> by 6 May, he had recovered.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Honours">Honours</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Honours">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_2">Club</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Paulo_Dybala&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Club">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Palermo</b><sup id="cite_ref-SW_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-21">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Serie_B" title="Serie B">Serie B</a>: <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Serie_B" title="2013–14 Serie B">2013–14</a><sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<p><b>Juventus</b><sup id="cite_ref-SW_21-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-21">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
